Upload and open 2D DWG drawings directly from hard disk drive, email or external storage and view all aspects of your DWG file, including external references, layers, and image underlays. Upgrade to AutoCAD mobile Premium to enable editing and drawings tools. Whether working online or offline, in the office or in the field, design every detail, everywhere. \r\n\r\nWhether you want to draft, view or mark up a DWG file, AutoCAD mobile has the plan that’s right for you. \r\n\r\nFeatures:\r\n\r\n• Free Premium trial for new users with absolutely no obligation\r\n• Open and view your DWG files\r\n• Measure accurately while on site\r\n• Use multi-touch zoom and pan to easily navigate large drawing\r\n• Work offline and sync your changes once back online\r\n• External cloud storage connectivity - View drawings from Google Drive, Dropbox, OneDrive, and more\r\n• Share your designs with others directly from mobile \r\n• Plot designs to PDF and share them via email\r\n• Download designs as DWG or DXF or PDF to your local hard disk drive \r\n• Use paper mark-ups\r\n• Advanced annotation tools, including: cloud, mark up, arrow and more! \r\n• Advanced layer management \r\n• View and edit object properties\r\n• Block palette containing all the Cinebench scores are used by system administrators to help make purchase decisions, journalists to review hardware, hardware manufacturers to optimize their latest products, as well as computer owners to evaluate their individual system. \r\n\r\nImprovements to Cinebench Release 20 reflect the overall advancements to CPU and rendering technology in recent years, providing a more accurate measurement of Cinema 4D's ability to take advantage of multiple CPU cores and modern processor features available to the average user.\r\n\r\nCinebench R20 FAQs:\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 uses a much larger and more complex test scene than R15 requiring about 8x the computational power needed to render it.
